Business Core Services: Finance, HR, Ops, Marketing, Sales, Product, Value Chain, Digital Workspace

Corporate Governance: M&A, IPOs, shareholder management, company entities

AI Analytics & Recommendation Engine: Insights, KPIs, predictive analytics

Developer API & Integrations: REST/gRPC, webhooks, SDK

Collaboration & Networking: Chats, meetings, notifications, shared workspaces, inter-org communications

Master Data & Enterprise Data: MDM, analytics, secure compliance

6. Event Schemas
{
  "event_type": "workflow_step_completed",
  "workflow_id": "wf_123",
  "step_id": "step_1",
  "status": "completed",
  "timestamp": "2025-11-29T12:00:00Z"

7. Database Schema (High-Level)
Tables:
- Organizations (id, name, type, lifecycle_stage)
- Users (id, name, role, org_id)
- Roles (id, name, permissions)
- Employees (id, name, role, department, org_id)
- Payments (id, amount, currency, org_id)
- FundingEvents (id, type, source, amount, org_id)
- Workflows (id, name, steps, status, org_id)
- MasterData (key, value, org_id)
- Deals (id, name, type, org_id, status)
- AIInsights (id, workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp)
8. API Specification (Sample)
paths:
  /orgs:
    post:
      summary: Create Organization
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/Organization'
      responses:
        '201': { description: Organization created }

  /finance/payment:
    post:
      summary: Process a payment
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/Payment'
      responses:
        '200': { description: Payment processed }

  /workflow/execute:
    post:
      summary: Execute workflow
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/Workflow'
      responses:
        '200': { description: Workflow executed }

M&A Deal Execution: Governance → Workflow orchestration → AI recommendations → Stakeholder approvals

1. API Endpoint Reference
Module	Endpoint	Method	Description	Example Payload
Platform Kernel	/health	GET	Health check	N/A
Platform Kernel	/orgs	POST	Create organization	{"name": "Acme Corp", "type": "operating"}
Platform Kernel	/users	POST	Create user	{"name": "Alice", "role": "admin", "org_id": "org_001"}
Finance	/finance/payment	POST	Process payment	{"amount":5000,"currency":"USD","org_id":"org_001"}
Finance	/finance/funding	POST	Add funding event	{"type":"VC","amount":1000000,"org_id":"org_001"}
HR	/employees	POST	Onboard employee	{"name":"Bob","role":"Engineer","department":"R&D"}
Workflow	/workflow/execute	POST	Execute workflow	{"workflow_id":"wf_123"}
AI Analytics	/ai/predict	POST	Generate insight	{"workflow_id":"wf_123","input":"sales_forecast"}
Collaboration	/chat/send	POST	Send chat message	{"workspace_id":"ws_001","message":"Hello Team!"}
Governance	/deals	POST	Initiate M&A deal	{"name":"Acquisition of X","type":"M&A"}
Governance	/ipo	POST	Start IPO process	{"org_id":"org_001","shares":1000000}

3. Database Queries – Quick Reference
Check Organization Details:

SELECT * FROM organizations WHERE id = 'org_001';
Get Employee List:

SELECT id, name, role FROM employees WHERE org_id='org_001';
Fetch Workflow Status:

SELECT id, name, status FROM workflows WHERE org_id='org_001';
AI Insights Dashboard:

SELECT workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp FROM ai_insights WHERE org_id='org_001';
Payments & Funding:

SELECT * FROM payments WHERE org_id='org_001';
SELECT * FROM funding_events WHERE org_id='org_001';

pub fn predict_sales(input: &str) -> String {
    format!("Predicted sales for {}: $100,000", input)
}

pub fn workflow_recommendation(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Recommended next step for workflow {}: Review Finance", workflow_id)
}
5. Deployment & CI/CD Commands
# Build Rust services
cargo build --release

# Run Platform Kernel
cargo run --bin platform_kernel

# Run HR Service
cargo run --bin hr_service

# Docker Build
docker build -t orgos/kernel ./platform_kernel

# Docker Run
docker run -p 8000:8000 orgos/kernel

# Kubernetes Deployment
kubectl apply -f k8s/platform_kernel.yaml

# Monitor Logs
kubectl logs -f deployment/platform-kernel

# CI/CD (GitHub Actions example)
# .github/workflows/deploy.yaml
6. Quick-Start Bootstrapping Commands
# Create a new organization
curl -X POST http://localhost:8000/orgs \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"name":"Acme Corp","type":"operating"}'

# Add admin user
curl -X POST http://localhost:8000/users \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"name":"Alice","role":"admin","org_id":"org_001"}'

# Initialize default workflows
curl -X POST http://localhost:8000/workflow/execute \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"workflow_id":"wf_onboarding"}'
7. RBAC & Security References
Role	Permissions
Admin	Full platform access, user management, workflow control
Manager	Access business services, approve workflows, view AI insights
Employee	Access assigned workflows, collaborate, submit updates
Investor	View KPIs, deals, dashboards, restricted access to sensitive data
System	Service-to-service API access, event publishing/subscription
Notes:

All API endpoints enforce RBAC

Events are signed & timestamped for audit logs

GDPR/CCPA compliance built-in for employee and client data

8. Event-Driven Orchestration Reference
Workflow: Employee Onboarding
1. HR Service -> Create Employee
2. Workflow Engine -> Trigger 'employee_onboarded' event
3. Master Data Service -> Update MDM
4. AI Engine -> Recommend training modules
5. Notifications Service -> Notify manager and employee
Workflow: Funding Event
1. Finance Service -> Record funding
2. Workflow Engine -> Trigger 'funding_event' event
3. Governance Service -> Update shareholders
4. AI Engine -> Predict impact on KPIs
5. Dashboard -> Display updated metrics
9. Master Data & Enterprise Data Commands
-- Add new MDM entry
INSERT INTO master_data (key, value, org_id) VALUES ('department_RnD','Research and Development','org_001');

-- Update analytics flag
UPDATE master_data SET value='1' WHERE key='enable_sales_forecast_ai' AND org_id='org_001';
10. Collaboration & Networking Commands
# Send chat message
curl -X POST http://localhost:8000/chat/send \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"workspace_id":"ws_001","message":"Hello Team!"}'

# Schedule meeting
curl -X POST http://localhost:8000/meetings/schedule \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"workspace_id":"ws_001","title":"Weekly Sync","time":"2025-11-30T10:00:00Z"}'

2. Platform Kernel (Rust Service Skeleton)
// platform_kernel/src/main.rs
mod rbac;
mod security;
mod org_bootstrap;
mod config;

use warp::Filter;

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    let health = warp::path!("health").map(|| warp::reply::json(&"OK"));

    let routes = health;

    warp::serve(routes).run(([127,0,0,1], 8000)).await;
}
// rbac.rs
pub struct Role {
    pub name: String,
    pub permissions: Vec<String>,
}

pub fn check_permission(role: &Role, permission: &str) -> bool {
    role.permissions.contains(&permission.to_string())
}
// org_bootstrap.rs
pub fn create_org(name: &str, org_type: &str) -> String {
    format!("Org {} of type {} created", name, org_type)
}
3. Business Core Service Example (Finance)
// finance_service/src/main.rs
use warp::Filter;

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    let payment = warp::path!("payment")
        .and(warp::post())
        .map(|| warp::reply::json(&"Payment Processed"));

    let funding = warp::path!("funding")
        .and(warp::post())
        .map(|| warp::reply::json(&"Funding Event Recorded"));

    let routes = payment.or(funding);

    warp::serve(routes).run(([127,0,0,1], 8100)).await;
}
4. Workflow Engine Skeleton
// workflow_engine/src/orchestrator.rs
pub struct Workflow {
    pub id: String,
    pub steps: Vec<String>,
    pub status: String,
}

pub fn execute_workflow(workflow: &Workflow) {
    println!("Executing workflow: {}", workflow.id);
}
// workflow_engine/src/event_bus.rs
pub fn publish_event(event_type: &str, payload: &str) {
    println!("Event Published: {} -> {}", event_type, payload);
}
5. AI Analytics Skeleton
// ai_analytics/src/prediction_engine.rs
pub fn predict_sales(input: &str) -> String {
    format!("Predicted sales for {}: $100,000", input)
}

pub fn recommend_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Next recommended step for {}: Finance Review", workflow_id)
}
6. Master Data Service Skeleton
// master_data/src/mdm.rs
pub fn set_master_data(key: &str, value: &str) {
    println!("MDM Updated: {} = {}", key, value);
}

pub fn get_master_data(key: &str) -> String {
    format!("Value for {} retrieved", key)
}
7. Collaboration Service Skeleton
// collaboration/src/chat_service.rs
pub fn send_message(workspace_id: &str, message: &str) {
    println!("Message sent to {}: {}", workspace_id, message);
}
8. API Gateway Example
// api_gateway/src/main.rs
use warp::Filter;

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    let org_create = warp::path!("orgs")
        .and(warp::post())
        .map(|| warp::reply::json(&"Organization Created"));

    warp::serve(org_create).run(([127,0,0,1], 8001)).await;
}

10. Deployment Commands / CI/CD Skeleton

cargo build --release

# Run Platform Kernel
cargo run --bin platform_kernel

# Run Finance Service
cargo run --bin finance_service

# Docker build
docker build -t orgos/platform_kernel ./platform_kernel

# Kubernetes deploy example
kubectl apply -f k8s/platform_kernel.yaml
11. Bootstrapping New Organization (Command Example)
# Create organization
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/orgs \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"name":"Acme Corp","type":"operating"}'

# Create admin user
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/users \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"name":"Alice","role":"admin","org_id":"org_001"}'

# Initialize default workflows
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/workflow/execute \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"workflow_id":"wf_onboarding"}'

OrgOS – Ultimate Text-Based Mega Blueprint
1. Executive Summary
OrgOS is a unified, microservices-based, Rust-first enterprise operating system designed to manage the full lifecycle of any organization—whether for-profit, non-profit, trust, holding company, or foundation. It provides enterprise-grade capabilities for:

Organization bootstrapping & lifecycle management

Finance, HR, Operations, Marketing, Sales, Product, Value Chain

Governance, M&A, IPOs, shareholder management

Workflow orchestration, event-driven automation

AI analytics, predictions, and recommendations

Collaboration, networking, inter-org connectivity

Master Data Management (MDM) and enterprise data integration

Platform-level security, compliance, RBAC, and GRC

Goals: Deliver operational efficiency, AI-driven insights, organizational extensibility, and governance compliance.

2. System Overview
Platform Layers:

Organization Kernel

Bootstrapping, RBAC, platform administration, infrastructure, security, privacy, compliance, and lifecycle management.

Enterprise Integration & Extensibility

APIs, SDKs, developer tools, custom modules, system component templates, and 3rd party integrations.

Business Core Services

Finance, HR, Ops, Marketing, Sales, Product, Value Chain, Digital Workspace, collaboration, AI insights, and analytics.

Corporate Governance Services

Mergers & Acquisitions, IPOs, shareholder management, legal entity management, and company type support (holding, subsidiary, operating, IP, trusts, funds).

Workflow & Orchestration

Event-driven workflows, automated triggers, notifications, and AI-assisted recommendations.

AI Analytics & Recommendation Engine

KPI dashboards, predictions, insight generation, and decision support.

Master Data & Enterprise Data Management

Enterprise MDM, secure data storage, analytics integration, cross-service access, and inter-org data exchange.

Collaboration & Networking

Chats, meetings, appointments, shared workspaces, inter-org communication, and networked OS interactions.

3. Core User Personas
Persona	Goals
CEO / Founder	Governance, strategy, executive dashboards, KPIs
CFO / Finance Lead	Capital/funding management, payments, reports, KPIs
HR Manager	Employee lifecycle, onboarding, culture management
Operations Lead	Supply chain, process automation, value chain oversight
Marketing / Sales Lead	Campaigns, promotions, sales funnel, deal lifecycle
Developer / IT Admin	Custom modules, APIs, deployments, integrations
Investor / Board Member	KPI insights, deals, shareholder updates

5. System Modules Overview

Org bootstrapping, RBAC, security, GRC, lifecycle management, platform admin.

Business Core Services

Finance, HR, Ops, Marketing, Sales, Product, Value Chain, Digital Workspace.

Payments, orders, RFP/RFQ, asset & equity mgmt.

Corporate Governance

M&A, IPO, shareholder, entity mgmt, company type support, compliance.

Workflow & Orchestration

Event-driven automation, triggers, notifications, AI recommendations.

KPI dashboards, predictive analytics, workflow recommendations.

MDM, secure storage, cross-service access, analytics integration.

Collaboration & Networking

Chats, meetings, shared workspaces, inter-org OS networking.

6. Business Use Cases & User Journeys
Employee Onboarding:
HR Service → Workflow Engine → MDM → AI → Notifications → Dashboard

Funding Event:
Finance → Workflow → Governance → AI → Dashboard → Investors

M&A Deal:
Governance → Workflow → Analytics → Notifications → Shareholders → Reports

AI Insights:
Workflow Engine → Event → AI Engine → Recommendation → Dashboard → User Action

Workflows(id, name, steps, status, org_id)
MasterData(key, value, org_id)
Deals(id, name, type, org_id, status)
AIInsights(id, workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp)

3. Module Implementation Guide
3.1 Platform Kernel
Purpose: Organization bootstrapping, RBAC, platform admin, security.

File structure:

platform_kernel/
 ├─ src/
 │  ├─ main.rs
 │  ├─ rbac.rs
 │  ├─ security.rs
 │  ├─ org_bootstrap.rs
 │  └─ config.rs
Key Implementation Steps:

rbac.rs – define roles, permissions, and access checks.

security.rs – implement JWT auth, audit logging, encryption utilities.

org_bootstrap.rs – functions for creating organizations, initializing default workflows.

config.rs – load environment variables, database URLs, service ports.

main.rs – Warp-based HTTP server exposing platform kernel endpoints.

Example API Endpoint:

POST /orgs
{
  "name": "Acme Corp",
  "type": "operating"
}
3.2 Business Core Services
Finance Service
Process payments, manage funding, generate reports.

Event-driven: publishes funding_event to workflow engine.

Stubs:

fn process_payment(amount: f64) { println!("Payment processed: {}", amount); }
fn record_funding(source: &str, amount: f64) { println!("Funding recorded"); }
HR Service
Employee lifecycle, onboarding, role assignments.

Event-driven: publishes employee_onboarded.

Stubs:

fn onboard_employee(employee_id: &str) { println!("Employee onboarded: {}", employee_id); }
Marketing & Sales
Campaigns, deal lifecycle, promotions.

Event-driven triggers for AI recommendations.

3.3 Corporate Governance
M&A management

IPO lifecycle

Shareholder management

Company type support (holding, subsidiary, IP, fund, trust)

Event Example:

{
  "event_type": "ipo_initiated",
  "company_id": "comp_001",
  "shares": 1000000,
  "price_per_share": 25,
  "timestamp": "2025-11-29T14:00:00Z"
}
3.4 Workflow Engine & Orchestration
Defines workflows with steps.

Event bus to connect services.

Executes workflows and triggers AI recommendations.

Example:

struct Workflow { id: String, steps: Vec<String>, status: String }
fn execute_workflow(workflow: &Workflow) { println!("Executing {}", workflow.id); }
3.5 AI Analytics & Recommendation Engine
Predictive analytics: sales, funding, KPIs.

Recommendations for workflows or strategic actions.

Example:

fn recommend_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Next step for {}: Finance Review", workflow_id)
}
3.6 Master Data & Enterprise Data
Centralized storage for all org data.

MDM, data security, cross-service access.

Example:

fn set_master_data(key: &str, value: &str) { println!("MDM Updated: {}={}", key,value); }
3.7 Collaboration & Networking
Chat, meetings, appointments, shared workspaces.

Supports networking between multiple OrgOS instances.

Event-driven notifications.

4. Event Flow Example
Employee Onboarding:

HR creates employee record.

Workflow engine triggers onboarding workflow.

AI recommends role training.

Collaboration service sends welcome message.

Dashboard updates KPI metrics.

10. Security & GRC
RBAC checks on every endpoint.

Audit logs for all actions.

GDPR / SOC2 / ISO27001 compliance.

Data encryption at rest and in transit.

11. Developer Best Practices
Use event-driven architecture between services.

Separate services into modules for scalability.

Use Rust async runtime (Tokio) for non-blocking operations.

Use Warp or Actix-Web for HTTP API endpoints.

Dockerize each service for microservices deployment.

Connect services via message queues (Kafka / NATS).

12. KPIs & Monitoring
Workflow execution success rates.

AI recommendation acceptance.

Onboarding times.

Payment & funding processing times.

Collaboration activity metrics.

OrgOS Developer Implementation Guide (Rust)
1. Project Overview
OrgOS is a microservices-based enterprise operating system implemented in Rust. The platform supports:

Full organization lifecycle

Governance: M&A, IPO, shareholder management

Business core: Finance, HR, Sales, Marketing, Value Chain

Collaboration & inter-org networking

Workflow orchestration & AI recommendations

Security, privacy, compliance, RBAC, and GRC

Master Data Management & Enterprise Data

Platform extensibility and custom module integration

Key Design Principles:

Event-driven microservices: Each module communicates via events (Kafka/NATS).

Rust-first: High-performance, type-safe, async services.

Modular: Each business function is its own service.

Extensible: Add custom business apps via standard APIs.

2. Project Structure (Rust)
orgos/
├─ platform_kernel/
│   ├─ src/
│   │   ├─ main.rs
│   │   ├─ rbac.rs
│   │   ├─ security.rs
│   │   ├─ lifecycle.rs
│   │   └─ config.rs
├─ business_core/
│   ├─ finance_service/
│   │   └─ src/main.rs
│   ├─ hr_service/
│   │   └─ src/main.rs
│   ├─ marketing_service/
│   │   └─ src/main.rs
│   └─ sales_service/
│       └─ src/main.rs
├─ governance/
│   ├─ mergers_acquisitions/
│   ├─ ipo/
│   └─ shareholder_mgmt/
├─ workflow_engine/
│   └─ src/main.rs
├─ ai_engine/
│   └─ src/main.rs
├─ collaboration/
│   └─ src/main.rs
├─ master_data/
│   └─ src/main.rs
└─ common_libs/
    └─ src/utils.rs
3. Microservice Skeletons
3.1 Platform Kernel
// platform_kernel/src/main.rs
#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    println!("Platform Kernel Service Started");
    warp::serve(routes()).run(([127,0,0,1], 8001)).await;
}

fn routes() -> warp::filters::BoxedFilter<(impl warp::Reply,)> {
    warp::path("orgs")
        .and(warp::post())
        .map(|| "Organization Created")
        .boxed()
}
3.2 Finance Service
fn process_payment(amount: f64, org_id: &str) {
    println!("Payment of {} processed for org {}", amount, org_id);
}
3.3 HR Service
fn onboard_employee(emp_id: &str, org_id: &str) {
    println!("Employee {} onboarded in org {}", emp_id, org_id);
}
3.4 AI Engine
fn recommend_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Workflow {} next step: Finance Approval", workflow_id)
}
4. API Contracts
Service	Endpoint	Method	Request	Response
Platform Kernel	/orgs	POST	{name, type}	{org_id, status}
HR	/employees	POST	{name, role, org_id}	{employee_id, status}
Finance	/payment	POST	{amount, org_id}	{payment_id, status}
Workflow	/execute	POST	{workflow_id, org_id}	{status, next_step}
AI Engine	/predict	POST	{workflow_id}	{recommendation}
Collaboration	/chat/send	POST	{workspace_id, message}	{status}
Governance	/ipo	POST	{company_id, shares, price}	{ipo_id, status}
5. Event Schemas
Example: Employee Onboarded

{
  "event_type": "employee_onboarded",
  "employee_id": "emp_001",
  "org_id": "org_001",
  "timestamp": "2025-11-29T15:00:00Z"
}
Example: Funding Received

{
  "event_type": "funding_received",
  "org_id": "org_001",
  "amount": 500000,
  "source": "VC",
  "timestamp": "2025-11-29T15:30:00Z"
}
6. Database Patterns
PostgreSQL for structured data

Redis for workflow state & caching

Kafka/NATS for event-driven communication

Key Tables:

Organizations(id, name, type, lifecycle_stage)
Users(id, name, role, org_id)
Employees(id, name, role, department, org_id)
Payments(id, amount, currency, org_id)
FundingEvents(id, type, source, amount, org_id)
Workflows(id, name, steps, status, org_id)
MasterData(key, value, org_id)
AIInsights(id, workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp)
Deals(id, type, org_id, status)
Collaboration(id, messages, workspace_id, participants)
7. Deployment & CI/CD
Dockerfile example (for any service):

FROM rust:1.75
WORKDIR /usr/src/app
COPY . .
RUN cargo build --release
CMD ["./target/release/service_binary"]
Kubernetes Deployment Skeleton:

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: platform-kernel
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: platform-kernel
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: platform-kernel
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: kernel
        image: orgos/platform-kernel:latest
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8001
CI/CD Pipeline Steps:

Lint & format Rust code (cargo fmt, cargo clippy)

Run tests (cargo test)

Build Docker images

Push images to registry

Deploy via Helm / Kubernetes

8. Bootstrapping & Onboarding
Create Organization:

curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/orgs -d '{"name":"Acme Corp","type":"operating"}'
Create Admin User:

curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/users -d '{"name":"Alice","role":"admin","org_id":"org_001"}'
Start Workflow:

curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/workflow/execute -d '{"workflow_id":"wf_onboarding"}'
9. Developer Best Practices
Keep microservices small & domain-focused.

Use async Rust (Tokio/Actix-Web/Warp).

Event-driven architecture for inter-service communication.

Encrypt sensitive data at rest & in transit.

Separate CI/CD pipelines per service for independent deployability.

Maintain schema versioning for master data.

Use unit & integration tests for each module.

10. Scaling & Extensibility
New services (custom apps) integrate via standard API contracts.

AI Engine provides plug-in recommendation logic.

Collaboration & inter-org networking support multi-instance scaling.

Platform Kernel handles role-based access & governance across all modules.

This guide is fully developer-ready, providing:

Module skeletons

API & event contracts

DB schema

Deployment guidance

Bootstrapping

Integration & AI stubs

1. Executive Summary
ORGOS – ORGANIZATION OPERATING SYSTEM
-------------------------------------
Vision: Provide a unified, fully extensible, AI-driven platform
for organizations of any type to manage lifecycle, governance,
business operations, and collaboration in a single microservices-based system.

Highlights:
- Fully modular, event-driven microservices architecture (Rust-first)
- Supports For-profit, NPOs, Foundations, Holdings, Subsidiaries, Funds
- Full lifecycle management: Bootstrapping → Growth → M&A → IPO → Exit
- Integrated AI analytics, workflow automation, master data management
- Collaboration, inter-org networking, governance, compliance, RBAC
- Extensible with custom business modules and third-party integrations
2. Core User Personas
- Administrators: Manage org setup, users, roles, permissions
- Executives & Managers: Monitor KPIs, oversee workflows, run approvals
- Employees: Perform assigned tasks, access collaboration tools
- Investors & Shareholders: Track funding, deal lifecycle, shareholder reporting
- Developers: Extend OrgOS, build custom modules, integrate external systems
3. System Modules Overview
1. Organization Kernel
   - RBAC & Roles
   - Security, Privacy, Compliance & GRC
   - Lifecycle Management
   - Platform Administration & Configuration
2. Business Core Services
   - Finance, HR, Sales, Marketing, Product, Value Chain, Operations
3. Workflow Engine
   - Event-driven orchestration and automation
4. AI Analytics & Recommendation Engine
   - Predictive insights and recommendations
5. Collaboration & Networking
   - Chats, Meetings, Shared Workspaces, Inter-org connectivity
6. Governance
   - M&A, IPO, Shareholder Management, Company Types
7. Master Data / Enterprise Data Management
   - Centralized MDM for all services
8. Platform Extensibility
   - Custom apps, third-party integrations, developer API

6. API Contracts
POST /orgs            → Create organization
POST /users           → Create user
POST /employees       → Add employee
POST /finance/payment → Process payment
POST /workflow/execute → Trigger workflow
POST /ai/predict      → AI recommendation
POST /chat/send       → Send message
POST /ipo             → Launch IPO
POST /mna             → Initiate M&A
Example Request:

{
  "name": "Acme Corp",
  "type": "operating"
}
Example Response:

{
  "org_id": "org_001",
  "status": "created"
}
7. Database Schema (Simplified)
Organizations(id, name, type, lifecycle_stage)
Users(id, name, role, org_id)
Employees(id, name, role, department, org_id)
Payments(id, amount, currency, org_id)

Workflows(id, name, steps, status, org_id)

AIInsights(id, workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp)
Deals(id, type, org_id, status)
Collaboration(id, messages, workspace_id, participants)
8. Event Schemas
employee_onboarded: { event_type, employee_id, org_id, timestamp }
funding_received:   { event_type, org_id, amount, source, timestamp }
workflow_completed: { event_type, workflow_id, org_id, status, timestamp }
ipo_launched:       { event_type, company_id, shares, price, timestamp }
mna_initiated:      { event_type, org_id, target_org_id, timestamp }

11. AI & Workflow Integration Stubs
fn ai_predict(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Next step recommendation for workflow {}", workflow_id)
}

fn workflow_event_trigger(event_type: &str, payload: serde_json::Value) {
    println!("Event triggered: {} with payload {:?}", event_type, payload);
}
12. Developer Best Practices
- Microservice separation: Keep each domain isolated
- Async Rust: Use Tokio/Warp/Actix
- Event-driven: Publish & subscribe via Kafka/NATS
- Security first: Encrypt sensitive data & enforce RBAC
- CI/CD per service
- Schema versioning for MDM
- Unit & integration testing

1. Executive Summary
ORGOS – ORGANIZATION OPERATING SYSTEM
-------------------------------------
Vision: Provide a fully extensible, AI-driven, unified enterprise platform
for managing all aspects of organization lifecycle, governance, business operations, 
and inter-org collaboration in a single microservices-based system.

- Microservices-first architecture in Rust
- Supports For-profit, NPOs, Foundations, Holdings, Subsidiaries, Funds
- Full organization lifecycle: Bootstrapping → Growth → M&A → IPO → Exit
- Core business modules: Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales, Product, Operations, Value Chain
- Workflow orchestration & AI recommendations
- Master Data Management & Enterprise Data
- Security, Privacy, Compliance, RBAC, GRC
- Collaboration & inter-org networking
- Extensible: Custom business modules & third-party integrations
- Investor-ready governance and reporting capabilities
2. Core User Personas
- Administrators: Org setup, user roles, permissions
- Executives & Managers: Monitor KPIs, workflow approvals, financial oversight
- Employees: Execute assigned tasks, collaborate, access shared workspaces
- Investors & Shareholders: Track funding, deals, shareholder reports
- Developers: Extend OrgOS, build custom modules, integrate external systems

5. API Contracts (Selected)
Service	Endpoint	Method	Request	Response
Org Kernel	/orgs	POST	{name, type}	{org_id, status}
HR	/employees	POST	{name, role, org_id}	{employee_id, status}
Finance	/payment	POST	{amount, org_id}	{payment_id, status}
Workflow	/execute	POST	{workflow_id, org_id}	{status, next_step}
AI	/predict	POST	{workflow_id}	{recommendation}
Collaboration	/chat/send	POST	{workspace_id, message}	{status}
Governance	/ipo	POST	{company_id, shares, price}	{ipo_id, status}
Governance	/mna	POST	{org_id, target_org_id}	{deal_id, status}
6. Database Schema (Simplified)
Organizations(id, name, type, lifecycle_stage)
Users(id, name, role, org_id)
Employees(id, name, role, department, org_id)
Payments(id, amount, currency, org_id)
FundingEvents(id, type, source, amount, org_id)
Workflows(id, name, steps, status, org_id)
AIInsights(id, workflow_id, recommendation, timestamp)
Deals(id, type, org_id, status)
Collaboration(id, messages, workspace_id, participants)
MasterData(key, value, org_id)
7. Event Schemas
employee_onboarded: { event_type, employee_id, org_id, timestamp }
funding_received:   { event_type, org_id, amount, source, timestamp }
workflow_completed: { event_type, workflow_id, org_id, status, timestamp }
ipo_launched:       { event_type, company_id, shares, price, timestamp }
mna_initiated:      { event_type, org_id, target_org_id, timestamp }
8. Bootstrapping & Onboarding Commands
# Create organization
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/orgs -d '{"name":"Acme Corp","type":"operating"}'

# Create admin user
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/users -d '{"name":"Alice","role":"admin","org_id":"org_001"}'

# Start workflow
curl -X POST http://localhost:8001/workflow/execute -d '{"workflow_id":"wf_onboarding"}'
9. Deployment & CI/CD
# Dockerfile (example)
FROM rust:1.75
WORKDIR /usr/src/app
COPY . .
RUN cargo build --release
CMD ["./target/release/service_binary"]

# Kubernetes Deployment Skeleton
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: platform-kernel
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: platform-kernel
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: platform-kernel
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: kernel
        image: orgos/platform-kernel:latest
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8001
CI/CD Steps:

Lint & format Rust (cargo fmt, cargo clippy)

Run tests (cargo test)

Build Docker images

Push to registry

Deploy via Helm/K8s

10. AI & Workflow Integration
fn ai_predict(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("Next step recommendation for workflow {}", workflow_id)
}

fn workflow_event_trigger(event_type: &str, payload: serde_json::Value) {
    println!("Event triggered: {} with payload {:?}", event_type, payload);
}
11. Developer Best Practices
Microservice isolation & domain focus

Async Rust (Tokio/Warp/Actix)

Event-driven communication (Kafka/NATS)

Security first: RBAC, encryption, GRC

Independent CI/CD pipelines

Version-controlled schemas for MDM

Unit & integration testing per service

OrgOS Developer Implementation Guide
1. Organization Kernel Service
Purpose: Centralizes RBAC, platform administration, lifecycle management, security, compliance & GRC.

Rust Microservice Skeleton:

use warp::Filter;

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    // Health check endpoint
    let health = warp::path!("health").map(|| warp::reply::json(&"OrgOS Kernel Online"));

    // Create organization
    let create_org = warp::path!("orgs")
        .and(warp::post())
        .and(warp::body::json())
        .map(|org: OrgRequest| {
            // Stub: persist org to DB
            warp::reply::json(&OrgResponse {
                org_id: "org_001".to_string(),
                status: "created".to_string(),
            })
        });

    warp::serve(health.or(create_org))
        .run(([0, 0, 0, 0], 8001))
        .await;
}

#[derive(serde::Deserialize)]
struct OrgRequest { name: String, org_type: String }

#[derive(serde::Serialize)]
struct OrgResponse { org_id: String, status: String }
Event Hooks:

organization_created: { org_id, org_type, timestamp }
role_assigned: { user_id, role, org_id, timestamp }
lifecycle_updated: { org_id, stage, timestamp }
2. Workflow & Orchestration Engine
Purpose: Manages workflow automation across all modules.

Rust Skeleton:

fn trigger_workflow(workflow_id: &str, org_id: &str) {
    println!("Workflow {} triggered for org {}", workflow_id, org_id);
    // Event emission stub
    emit_event("workflow_triggered", workflow_id, org_id);
}

fn emit_event(event_type: &str, workflow_id: &str, org_id: &str) {
    println!("Event: {} for workflow {} in org {}", event_type, workflow_id, org_id);
}
Event Schema Example:

workflow_completed: { workflow_id, org_id, status, timestamp }
3. AI Analytics & Recommendations Engine
Purpose: Provide predictive analytics, workflow guidance, and recommendations.

Rust Skeleton:

fn predict_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("AI recommendation for workflow {}", workflow_id)
}

fn analyze_financial_risk(org_id: &str) -> f64 {
    // Stub: risk score 0.0 - 1.0
    0.42
}
Integration Points:

Workflow Engine → AI → Recommendations

Finance → AI → Cashflow risk alerts

HR → AI → Training recommendations

Governance → AI → M&A / IPO risk

4. Business Core Services
Modules & Endpoints:

Module	Endpoint	Method	Description
Finance	/payments	POST	Process payment
Finance	/funding	POST	Record funding event
HR	/employees	POST	Create employee
HR	/onboarding	POST	Start onboarding workflow
Marketing	/campaigns	POST	Launch campaign
Sales	/deals	POST	Create new deal
Product	/product	POST	Add/update product
Operations	/logistics	POST	Manage shipments & inventory
Rust Service Skeleton Example (HR):

warp::path!("employees")
    .and(warp::post())
    .and(warp::body::json())
    .map(|emp: Employee| {
        // persist to DB
        emit_event("employee_onboarded", &emp.id, &emp.org_id);
        warp::reply::json(&emp)
    });

#[derive(serde::Deserialize, serde::Serialize)]
struct Employee { id: String, name: String, role: String, org_id: String }
5. Governance & Lifecycle Module
Purpose: Manages M&A, IPOs, shareholder management, company types, and full org lifecycle.

Rust Skeleton Example:

fn launch_ipo(company_id: &str, shares: u32, price: f64) -> String {
    println!("IPO launched for company {}: {} shares @ {}", company_id, shares, price);
    "ipo_001".to_string()
}

fn initiate_mna(org_id: &str, target_org_id: &str) -> String {
    println!("M&A initiated between {} and {}", org_id, target_org_id);
    "mna_001".to_string()
}
Event Hooks:

ipo_launched: { company_id, shares, price, timestamp }
mna_initiated: { org_id, target_org_id, timestamp }
shareholder_added: { shareholder_id, org_id, shares, timestamp }
6. Collaboration & Networking Service
Purpose: Real-time messaging, shared workspace, notifications, inter-org networking.

fn send_message(workspace_id: &str, user_id: &str, msg: &str) {
    println!("User {} sent message in workspace {}: {}", user_id, workspace_id, msg);
}
Integration:

Workflow Engine triggers notifications

AI recommends meetings & alerts

Inter-org API allows secure message sharing

7. Master Data & Enterprise Data Management
Purpose: Central repository for enterprise-wide knowledge, investment, and analytics data.

Rust Skeleton:

struct MasterData { key: String, value: String, org_id: String }

fn store_data(md: MasterData) {
    println!("Stored master data {} for org {}", md.key, md.org_id);
}
Key Features:

MDM for consistent enterprise data

Supports AI & analytics engines

Events propagate to all modules on updates

8. Inter-Org Networking & API Gateway
Purpose: Allows secure inter-org communication and shared workflows.

fn send_interorg_event(org_from: &str, org_to: &str, event: &str) {
    println!("Inter-org event from {} to {}: {}", org_from, org_to, event);
}
Security: RBAC, encrypted API calls, GRC compliance

9. Deployment & CI/CD Example
# Build all Rust microservices
cargo build --release

# Dockerize
docker build -t orgos/kernel ./kernel
docker build -t orgos/workflow ./workflow
docker build -t orgos/ai ./ai
docker build -t orgos/hr ./hr

# Deploy via Kubernetes
kubectl apply -f deployments/kernel.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/workflow.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/ai.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/hr.yaml

# Monitor logs
kubectl logs -f deployment/kernel

ORGOS – ORGANIZATION OPERATING SYSTEM
Ultimate Text-Based Mega-Document

1. Executive Summary
OrgOS is a unified, AI-driven, microservices-based Organization Operating System, designed to manage the entire lifecycle of any organization—from bootstrapping and operations to M&A, IPOs, and inter-organizational networking.

Key Features:

Full lifecycle management: Startup → Growth → Acquisition → IPO → Exit

Supports multiple org types: For-profit, NPOs, Foundations, Holdings, Subsidiaries, Funds, Trusts

Modular, extensible architecture with custom business apps & workflow automation

Enterprise-grade RBAC, Security, GRC, and compliance built-in

AI-driven analytics, recommendations, and predictive insights

Master Data & Enterprise Knowledge Management

Collaboration, inter-org networking, and shared workspaces

M&A, IPO, funding, shareholder, and value chain management

Value Proposition:

Reduces operational complexity across multiple departments and subsidiaries

Automates workflows with AI recommendations

Provides a unified view of data, performance, and strategic initiatives

Enables secure collaboration and data exchange between organizations

2. System Overview
Core Microservice Modules:

Organization Kernel: RBAC, Platform Admin, Security/GRC, Lifecycle

Workflow & Orchestration Engine: Event-driven automation, workflow templates

AI Analytics & Recommendations Engine: Predictive insights for Finance, HR, Ops, Governance

Business Core Services: Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales, Product, Operations

Governance & Lifecycle: M&A, IPO, shareholder management, company types, org lifecycle

Collaboration & Networking: Chat, notifications, shared workspace, inter-org network

Master Data & Enterprise Data Management: MDM, analytics, knowledge repository

External OrgOS Network: Inter-org communication and workflow sharing

Architecture Principles:

Fully microservices-based

Event-driven with Kafka/NATS or equivalent

Rust-based services for performance, safety, and concurrency

Modular and extensible for custom modules and third-party integrations

CI/CD pipelines with Docker/Kubernetes deployments

AI integration points across all workflows and business modules

3. Core User Personas
Executives: Track KPIs, approve funding, strategic decision-making

Managers: Oversee department operations, approve workflows

Employees: Execute tasks, collaborate, access training

Investors & Shareholders: Track funding, IPOs, and performance metrics

Administrators: Configure platform, RBAC, security, and compliance

External Partners: Collaborate via inter-org networking

5. Module-by-Module Developer Guide
Organization Kernel
Responsibilities: RBAC, lifecycle management, platform admin, security, GRC

Event Hooks: organization_created, role_assigned, lifecycle_updated

Rust Skeleton:

// Organization Kernel service
Workflow Engine
Manages automation & orchestration

Event Hooks: workflow_triggered, workflow_completed

Rust stub provided

AI Analytics Engine
Predictive recommendations

Event Hooks: risk_alert, workflow_advice

Business Core Services
Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales, Product, Ops

Each microservice exposes REST endpoints and emits workflow events

Governance & Lifecycle
M&A, IPOs, shareholder mgmt, org lifecycle

Event Hooks: ipo_launched, mna_initiated, shareholder_added

Collaboration & Networking
Chat, notifications, shared workspace

Event Hooks: message_sent, workspace_updated

Master Data & MDM
Centralized repository for analytics and knowledge

Event Hooks: data_updated, mdm_synced

External OrgOS Network
Inter-org event exchange

Secured API and workflow integration

6. Database Schema (Simplified)
tables:
- organizations: id, name, type, status, created_at
- users: id, name, role, org_id, created_at
- employees: id, name, role, org_id
- workflows: id, org_id, type, status
- workflow_events: id, workflow_id, type, timestamp
- funding_events: id, org_id, source, amount, timestamp
- ipos: id, company_id, shares, price, date
- mnas: id, org_id, target_org_id, status, date
- master_data: key, value, org_id
7. API Endpoints Catalog (Example)
POST /orgs                → create organization
POST /users               → create user
POST /employees           → onboard employee
POST /workflows           → trigger workflow
GET  /workflows/:id       → workflow status
POST /finance/payments    → create payment
POST /funding             → record funding event
POST /governance/ipo      → launch IPO
POST /governance/mna      → initiate M&A
POST /collaboration/msg   → send message
POST /masterdata          → store master data

ORGOS – Operational Playbook & Cheat Sheet (Text-Based)
1. Developer Quick Start Commands
Build & Run Rust Microservices

# Build all services
cargo build --release

# Dockerize services
docker build -t orgos/kernel ./kernel
docker build -t orgos/workflow ./workflow
docker build -t orgos/ai ./ai
docker build -t orgos/hr ./hr

# Run locally for testing
cargo run --bin kernel
cargo run --bin workflow
cargo run --bin ai
cargo run --bin hr

# Deploy via Kubernetes
kubectl apply -f deployments/kernel.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/workflow.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/ai.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/hr.yaml

# Monitor logs
kubectl logs -f deployment/kernel
kubectl logs -f deployment/workflow
2. Event Flow Cheat Sheet
EVENT: organization_created
Payload: { org_id, org_type, timestamp }

EVENT: role_assigned
Payload: { user_id, role, org_id, timestamp }

EVENT: workflow_triggered
Payload: { workflow_id, org_id, type, timestamp }

EVENT: workflow_completed
Payload: { workflow_id, org_id, status, timestamp }

EVENT: ipo_launched
Payload: { company_id, shares, price, timestamp }

EVENT: mna_initiated
Payload: { org_id, target_org_id, timestamp }

EVENT: employee_onboarded
Payload: { employee_id, org_id, timestamp }

EVENT: message_sent
Payload: { workspace_id, user_id, message, timestamp }
3. API Endpoint Stubs (Quick Reference)
Module	Endpoint	Method	Purpose
Kernel	/orgs	POST	Create organization
Kernel	/users	POST	Create user / assign role
HR	/employees	POST	Onboard employee
Workflow	/workflows	POST	Trigger workflow
Workflow	/workflows/:id	GET	Get workflow status
Finance	/finance/payments	POST	Process payment
Finance	/funding	POST	Record funding event
Governance	/governance/ipo	POST	Launch IPO
Governance	/governance/mna	POST	Initiate M&A
Collaboration	/collaboration/msg	POST	Send message
Master Data	/masterdata	POST	Store or update enterprise data
4. Deployment & CI/CD Cheat Sheet
# Build Rust services
cargo build --release

# Dockerize services
docker build -t orgos/<service> ./<service>

# Push to registry
docker push orgos/kernel
docker push orgos/workflow
docker push orgos/ai
docker push orgos/hr

# Kubernetes deployment
kubectl apply -f deployments/kernel.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/workflow.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/ai.yaml
kubectl apply -f deployments/hr.yaml

# Check pod status
kubectl get pods

# Tail logs for monitoring
kubectl logs -f deployment/kernel
kubectl logs -f deployment/workflow

// AI Predictive Recommendation Stub
fn predict_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("AI Recommendation for workflow {}", workflow_id)
}

// Financial risk analysis stub
fn analyze_financial_risk(org_id: &str) -> f64 {
    0.42 // placeholder risk score
}
Integration Points:

Workflow Engine → AI → Recommendations

Finance → AI → Risk alerts

HR → AI → Training suggestions

Governance → AI → M&A/IPO advice

6. Master Data & MDM Quick Commands
struct MasterData { key: String, value: String, org_id: String }

fn store_data(md: MasterData) {
    println!("Stored master data {} for org {}", md.key, md.org_id);
}
Event Hook: data_updated → triggers sync across all modules

Employee Onboarding Workflow:

Step 1: Create Employee Record
Step 2: Assign Role & Access
Step 3: Schedule Orientation (AI recommendation)
Step 4: Assign Workstation / Tools
Step 5: Launch Training Modules
Step 6: Complete Workflow
Events Triggered:

employee_onboarded → workflow_triggered → workflow_completed → AI Insights

ORGOS – Developer Implementation Playbook (Text-Based)
1. Project Structure
orgos/
├── kernel/                # Organization Kernel
├── workflow/              # Workflow & Orchestration Engine
├── ai/                    # AI Analytics & Recommendation Engine
├── business_core/         # Finance, HR, Ops, Marketing, Sales
├── governance/            # Lifecycle, M&A, IPO, Shareholder Management
├── collaboration/         # Chat, Notifications, Shared Workspaces
├── mdm/                   # Master Data & Enterprise Knowledge
├── inter_org/             # External OrgOS Networking
├── api_gateway/           # API & Extensibility Layer
├── deployments/           # Docker/Kubernetes configs
├── scripts/               # Helper scripts for deployment and testing
└── docs/                  # Documentation, diagrams, cheat sheets
2. Module-by-Module Rust Skeletons
2.1 Organization Kernel
// src/main.rs
use actix_web::{web, App, HttpServer, Responder};

async fn create_org() -> impl Responder {
    "Organization Created"
}

async fn assign_role() -> impl Responder {
    "Role Assigned"
}

#[actix_web::main]
async fn main() -> std::io::Result<()> {
    HttpServer::new(|| {
        App::new()
            .route("/orgs", web::post().to(create_org))
            .route("/users", web::post().to(assign_role))
    })
    .bind("127.0.0.1:8080")?
    .run()
    .await
}
Events:

organization_created
role_assigned
lifecycle_updated
2.2 Workflow Engine
fn trigger_workflow(workflow_id: &str) {
    println!("Workflow {} triggered", workflow_id);
    // Emit event workflow_triggered
}

fn complete_workflow(workflow_id: &str) {
    println!("Workflow {} completed", workflow_id);
    // Emit event workflow_completed
}
Event Hooks: workflow_triggered, workflow_completed, workflow_failed

2.3 AI Analytics Engine
fn predict_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String {
    format!("AI Suggestion for workflow {}", workflow_id)
}

fn risk_analysis(org_id: &str) -> f64 {
    0.42 // Placeholder risk score
}
Integration points: workflow automation, finance, HR, governance modules

2.4 Business Core Services (Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales, Operations)
fn create_payment(org_id: &str, amount: f64) {
    println!("Payment of {} created for org {}", amount, org_id);
}

fn onboard_employee(emp_id: &str, org_id: &str) {
    println!("Employee {} onboarded in org {}", emp_id, org_id);
}

fn create_marketing_campaign(org_id: &str, campaign_name: &str) {
    println!("Campaign '{}' created for org {}", campaign_name, org_id);
}
2.5 Governance & Lifecycle Module
fn launch_ipo(company_id: &str, shares: u32, price: f64) {
    println!("IPO launched for company {} with {} shares at ${}", company_id, shares, price);
}

fn initiate_mna(org_id: &str, target_org_id: &str) {
    println!("M&A initiated between {} and {}", org_id, target_org_id);
}

fn update_shareholder(org_id: &str, shareholder_id: &str) {
    println!("Shareholder {} updated for org {}", shareholder_id, org_id);
}
2.6 Collaboration & Communication Module
fn send_message(workspace_id: &str, user_id: &str, message: &str) {
    println!("User {} sent message in workspace {}: {}", user_id, workspace_id, message);
}

fn schedule_meeting(meeting_id: &str, participants: Vec<&str>) {
    println!("Meeting {} scheduled with {:?}", meeting_id, participants);
}
2.7 Master Data & MDM Module
struct MasterData {
    key: String,
    value: String,
    org_id: String,
}

fn store_data(md: MasterData) {
    println!("Stored master data {} for org {}", md.key, md.org_id);
    // Emit data_updated event
}
2.8 External OrgOS Network
fn connect_org(remote_org_id: &str) {
    println!("Connected to external OrgOS: {}", remote_org_id);
}

fn sync_workflow_with_external(workflow_id: &str, remote_org_id: &str) {
    println!("Workflow {} synced with org {}", workflow_id, remote_org_id);
}
3. Event Flow Overview
organization_created → assign_role → workflow_triggered → AI Prediction → workflow_completed → KPI Update → Master Data Update
ipo_launched → shareholder_updated → financial_metrics → investor_dashboard
mna_initiated → AI Recommendations → integration workflow → master_data_sync
employee_onboarded → assign_workstation → training_scheduled → workflow_completed
4. Deployment & CI/CD
# Build Rust services
cargo build --release

# Dockerize each service
docker build -t orgos/kernel ./kernel
docker build -t orgos/workflow ./workflow
docker build -t orgos/ai ./ai
docker build -t orgos/business_core ./business_core

# Deploy on Kubernetes

5. API Contracts Example
POST /orgs – Create Organization
Request:

{
  "name": "Acme Corp",
  "type": "Operating Company"
}
Response:

{
  "org_id": "org_12345",
  "status": "created"
}
POST /workflows – Trigger Workflow
Request:

{
  "workflow_type": "employee_onboarding",
  "org_id": "org_12345"
}

Use Postman / cURL to test APIs

Use Prometheus + Grafana for real-time metrics

Centralized logging with ELK stack

AI engine provides predictive recommendations for workflows, finance, HR, governance

Master Data & MDM module ensures consistent enterprise-wide data

External OrgOS network enables inter-organization workflows

Rust chosen for safety, concurrency, and performance across all microservices

ORGOS – Ultimate Text-Based Blueprint Document

1. Executive Summary
OrgOS is a full-featured Organization Operating System.

Supports For-Profit, Non-Profit, Foundations, Subsidiaries, Funds, Trusts.

Enables organization lifecycle management, including bootstrapping, governance, M&A, IPOs, shareholder management.

Provides AI-powered insights for workflow automation, predictive analytics, and risk analysis.

Event-driven Rust microservices architecture, fully extensible with custom modules and third-party integrations.

2. System Overview
Modular, microservices-based architecture.

Event-driven design for workflows, AI insights, and master data.

Fully integrated collaboration, business core, governance, lifecycle, and inter-org networking modules.

Extensible via API gateway and developer portal.

3. Core User Personas
Executives: Decision-making, KPI dashboards, lifecycle oversight.

Managers: Workflow approval, team management, reporting.

Employees: Task execution, collaboration, onboarding.

Investors / Shareholders: Portfolio insights, funding lifecycle, ROI.

Developers / Admins: Module integration, custom workflow creation, API access.

5. System Modules Overview
Organization Kernel: RBAC, security, lifecycle, platform administration

Workflow Engine: Event-driven orchestration, automation hooks

AI Engine: Predictions, recommendations, risk scoring

Business Core: Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales, Operations, Product

Governance: IPO, M&A, shareholder management, company types

Collaboration: Chat, notifications, shared workspaces, meetings

Inter-Org Networking: Cross-organization workflow integration

Master Data / MDM: Enterprise-wide data consistency

API & Extensibility: Custom modules, 3rd-party tool integrations

6. Developer Implementation Playbook (Module Skeletons)
Kernel (Rust)
async fn create_org() -> impl Responder { "Organization Created" }
async fn assign_role() -> impl Responder { "Role Assigned" }
Workflow
fn trigger_workflow(id: &str) { println!("Triggered workflow {}", id); }
fn complete_workflow(id: &str) { println!("Completed workflow {}", id); }
AI Engine
fn predict_next_step(workflow_id: &str) -> String { format!("AI Suggestion for {}", workflow_id) }
fn risk_analysis(org_id: &str) -> f64 { 0.42 }
Business Core
fn create_payment(org_id: &str, amount: f64) {}
fn onboard_employee(emp_id: &str, org_id: &str) {}
Governance
fn launch_ipo(company_id: &str, shares: u32, price: f64) {}
fn initiate_mna(org_id: &str, target_org_id: &str) {}
Collaboration
fn send_message(workspace_id: &str, user_id: &str, message: &str) {}
fn schedule_meeting(meeting_id: &str, participants: Vec<&str>) {}
Master Data / MDM
struct MasterData { key: String, value: String, org_id: String }
fn store_data(md: MasterData) {}
External OrgOS
fn connect_org(remote_org_id: &str) {}
fn sync_workflow_with_external(workflow_id: &str, remote_org_id: &str) {}
7. API Endpoints (Sample)
POST /orgs → Create organization
POST /users → Assign role
POST /workflows → Trigger workflow
GET /ai/predict → Get AI recommendation
POST /payments → Finance transactions
POST /ipo → Launch IPO
POST /mna → Initiate M&A
POST /messages → Collaboration message
8. Event & Workflow Schemas
organization_created
role_assigned
workflow_triggered
workflow_completed
risk_alert
data_updated
ipo_launched
shareholder_updated
mna_initiated
employee_onboarded
9. Business Use Cases / User Journeys
New Org Bootstrapping: Org creation → Assign roles → Onboard employees → Setup workflows → Launch first business process

IPO Lifecycle: Shareholder mgmt → Legal compliance → IPO launch → Investor reporting

M&A Process: Target identification → AI due diligence → Workflow orchestration → Integration → Master data sync

Daily Operations: Finance, HR, Marketing, Sales → AI recommendations → Workflow execution → KPI updates

10. Data Model Overview
Org: id, name, type, lifecycle_stage

User: id, name, role, org_id

Workflow: id, type, org_id, status

AI Recommendation: id, workflow_id, prediction, confidence

MasterData: key, value, org_id

Transaction / Payment: id, org_id, amount, status

IPO / M&A: id, org_id, status, date

15. Deployment & CI/CD Guide
# Build Rust microservices
cargo build --release

# Dockerize services
docker build -t orgos/kernel ./kernel
docker build -t orgos/workflow ./workflow

# Kubernetes deployment
kubectl apply -f deployments/

# Monitor logs
kubectl logs -f deployment/kernel
16. Security Architecture
RBAC enforced at kernel level

Data encrypted in transit (TLS) & at rest (AES-256)

Audit logs on workflows & financial transactions

Compliance hooks (GDPR, SOC2, ISO) integrated in governance module

17. End-User Manuals / Cheat Sheets
Creating a New Org: /orgs POST {name, type}

Trigger Workflow: /workflows POST {workflow_type, org_id}

Check AI Recommendation: /ai/predict GET?workflow_id=xyz

Launch IPO: /ipo POST {company_id, shares, price}

Send Message: /messages POST {workspace_id, user_id, message}

Legend / Flow Notes
Vertical Arrows (│, ▼): Data & workflow propagation

Horizontal Arrows (───>): Event-driven triggers between modules

Events Examples:

organization_created, role_assigned, workflow_triggered, workflow_completed

data_updated, risk_alert, ipo_launched, shareholder_updated

mna_initiated, employee_onboarded, workflow_synced

AI Integration: AI engine monitors workflows, finance, HR, governance, providing predictions & recommendations that feed back into workflow engine.

Master Data / MDM: Central repository for enterprise-wide data; synchronized with all modules and inter-org connections.

Inter-Org Networking: Enables cross-organization workflows, collaboration, and shared analytics.

Platform Extensibility: Developer API for custom modules, third-party integrations, and orchestration hooks.

Workflow Example Overlay
New Org Bootstrapping:
users_create → kernel_setup → assign_roles → workflow_triggered → ai_recommend → workflow_completed → mdm_sync → collaboration_ready
IPO Process:
kernel_check → governance_ipo → ai_risk_analysis → workflow_triggered → shareholder_updated → business_core_finance → mdm_sync → reporting
M&A Process:
target_identified → ai_due_diligence → workflow_triggered → governance_approval → master_data_sync → inter-org_sync → integration_complete
